CHAPTER III 
GENERAL INFORMATION RELATING TO THE FUND  
TDA 22-MIXTO 
III.1.  Legal information and Purpose of the Creation of the Fund 
“TDA 22-MIXTO, Fondo de Titulización de Activos” is incorporated pursuant to the 
provisions of Royal Decree 926/1998. The Fund is regulated in agreement with (i) the present 
Issue Prospectus; (ii) the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund, (iii) Royal Decree 926/1998 and 
subsequent provisions, (iv) Law 19/1992, for aspects not covered by Royal Decree 926/1998 
when applicable, (v) Law 24/1988, in its current wording in respect to supervision, inspection 
and sanction, and where applicable and, (vi) any other legal provisions in force at each time 
where applicable.  
The sole purpose of the Fund is the transformation of a series of Mortgage Loans through 
Shares and Certificates acquired from credit institutions into fixed income homogeneous, 
standardised, securities, and susceptible of being negotiated in organised securities markets. 
III.2.  Name, Incorporation and Registration of the Fund 
A prerequisite for the incorporation of the Fund and the issue of the Bonds is its registration in 
the Official Registry of the CNMV, pursuant to article 5 (3) of Royal Decree 926/1998.  
Once the Prospectus has been registered with the CNMV and before the opening of the 
Subscription Period, the Sociedad Gestora, together with the Sellers of the Shares and 
Certificates to be included in the Fund, will proceed to grant the Deed of Incorporation of the 
Fund under the terms set out in Royal Decree 926/1998. 
The Deed of Incorporation will comply with article 6 of Law 24/1988 and will, therefore, be 
the Deed of issue of the Securities and the Deed setting forth the representation of the 
Securities as book entries.  
The Deed of Incorporation, pursuant to article 5 (4) of Royal Decree 926/1998, will not be 
subject to registration in the Commercial Registry. 
III.3.  Management and Representation of the Fund and the Bond holders 
III.3.1. 
Functions and Responsibilities of the Sociedad Gestora 
"TDA 22-MIXTO, Fondo de Titulización de Activos" has been arranged by "Titulización de 
Activos, SGFT, S.A." as Sociedad Gestora empowered for such purpose, and, therefore, to 
administer and legally represent the Fund TDA 22-MIXTO, in accordance with the 
provisions of Royal Decree 926/1998. 
The Sociedad Gestora, as manager of third-party business, will represent and defend the 
interests of the holders of the Securities issued by the Fund.

The holders of the Securities will have no legal recourse against the Sociedad Gestora 
except if the Sociedad Gestora is in breach of its obligations as set out in the Deed of 
Incorporation of the Fund, in the present Prospectus and in applicable law. 
For information purposes only, and without prejudice to other actions provided in the Deed 
of incorporation and in this Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora will, in particular, be 
responsible for the following duties: 
(i) 
Ensuring that the amount of the payments effectively received by the Fund 
corresponds to the amount contractually due to the Fund, in accordance with the 
relevant contracts from which such payments arise. If necessary, the Sociedad 
Gestora will exercise all judicial and extra-judicial actions necessary or convenient 
to enforce and protect the rights of the Fund and the holders of the Securities. 
(ii) 
Applying any amount received by the Fund to the payment of its obligations, in 
accordance with the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund and this Prospectus. 
(iii) 
Extending or modifying any agreements entered into on behalf of the Fund and 
necessary to its operation, in accordance with the provisions of the Deed of 
Incorporation, this Prospectus and applicable law from time to time. All of the above 
shall be without prejudice to its giving notice to the Rating Agency and the CNMV, 
provided that the interests of the holders of the Securities are not adversely affected.  
(iv) 
Replacing all service providers of the Fund, in the terms provided in the Deed of 
Incorporation of the Fund and this Prospectus, provided that this is permitted by 
applicable law, that prior authorisation from the relevant authorities is obtained if 
necessary, that notice is given to the Rating Agency, and that the interests of the 
holders of the Securities are not impaired. In particular, in the event of breach of the 
duties of the Sellers of the Mortgage Loans, the Sociedad Gestora will take all 
measures necessary to obtain an adequate servicing of the Loans. 
(v) 
Giving all necessary instructions to the Financial Agent in relation to the Accounts 
of the Fund.  
(vi) 
Giving all necessary instructions to the Financial Agent in relation to the payments 
to be made to the holders of the Securities and if necessary, to all other entities to 
which such payments should be made. 
(vii) 
Determining and effecting payments regarding the principal and interest of the 
Loans (Initial Expenses Loan 1, 2 and Subordinated Loans 1 and 2, and Participating 
Loans 1 and 2). 
(viii) 
Appointing and, if necessary, replacing the Auditor, with the prior authorisation of 
the CNMV. 
(ix) 
Drafting and submitting to the relevant bodies all documents and information that 
must be submitted in accordance with applicable law and the present Prospectus, to 
the CNMV and drafting and submitting to the holders of the Securities any 
information legally required.

III.3.2. 
Remuneration of the Sociedad Gestora 
The Sociedad Gestora will receive, on each Payment Date, a management fee which will 
accrue quarterly, equal to a fixed amount of 18,750 Euro plus 1/4 of 0.0320% of the 
Outstanding Nominal Balance pending maturity of the Shares and Certificates on the 
immediately preceding Payment Date. Such fee will be understood in gross terms, 
including, therefore, any direct or indirect tax or withholding that may be applicable thereto. 
Said fixed amount will be updated at the beginning of each calendar year in accordance with 
the General Consumer Price Index published by the National Statistics Institute, or the 
entity which should replace it. On the first Payment Date, the management fee shall be 
calculated, not as ¼ of the resulting amount (equivalent to one quarter) but according to the 
number of days elapsed since the Disbursement Date.

(i) 
The Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Shares and Certificates.

accrued and unpaid in respect of Payment IO-1 and Payment IO-2.

III.4.4. 
Resources of the Fund derived from its operation 
The Fund will have two types of available resources, depending on the Mortgage Loans 
from which they are originated: Available Resources 1 and Available Resources 2. 
Available Resources 1: 
The Available Resources 1 of the Fund on each Payment Date will be equal to the sum of: 
(i) 
The balance of the Treasury Account originating from Mortgage Shares, composed 
of (a) any amount corresponding to the Mortgage Shares included in the Fund; (b) 
amounts at each given time of the Reserve Fund 1 and (c) the returns generated by 
said balance. 
(ii) 
As the case may be, the balance of the Reinvestment Accounts originating from 
Mortgage Shares, including the returns generated, except for the amount of 
principal and interest which do not correspond to the three Calculation Periods 
preceding the current Payment Date. 
(iii) 
Furthermore, as the case may be and when it is expedient, the proceeds of the 
Liquidation of the Fund’s Assets and the balance of the Collection Account, 
originating from the Mortgage Shares, including returns thereof. 
Available Resources 2: 
Available Resources 2 of the Fund on each Payment Date will be equal to the sum of: 
(i) 
The balance of the Treasury Account originating from the Mortgage Transfer 
Certificates, composed of (a) any amount corresponding to the Mortgage Transfer 
Certificates included in the Fund; (b) amounts of the Reserve Fund 2 at any given 
time and (c) the returns generated by said balance. 
(ii) 
If applicable, the balance of the Reinvestment Accounts originating from the 
Mortgage Transfer Certificates, including the returns generated, except for the 
amount of principal and interest which do not correspond to the three Calculation 
Periods preceding the current Payment Date. 
(iii) 
Furthermore, as the case may be and when it is expedient, the proceeds of the 
Liquidation of the Fund’s Assets and the balance of the Collection Account, 
originating from the Mortgage Transfer Certificates, including returns thereof.

III.5.3. 
Obligation to Notify Relevant Facts 
The Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, undertakes to report immediately to the 
CNMV, the Rating Agency and to the holders of the Securities, and throughout the life of 
the issue, any relevant event that may occur relating to the Shares and Certificates, to the 
Securities, to the Fund and to the Sociedad Gestora itself, that might have major impact on 
the trading of the Securities, and, in particular, the amount payable to the holders of the 
Securities, on every Payment Date, on account of principal and interest and as Payment IO-
1 and Payment IO-2, as provided in sections II.12. of this Prospectus, and, in general, any 
relevant modification of the assets or liabilities of the Fund. 
III.6.  Taxation of the Fund 
Please find below a brief extract of the applicable tax regime applicable to the Fund: 
 a) 
Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates 
Payments made to the Fund on account of interest on the Shares and Certificates, loans or other 
rights of credit that constitute income to securitization funds, are exempt from withholding in 
accordance with article 59 k) of Royal Decree 1777/2004, of July 30. 
In the event that in the future any direct or indirect tax, charges or withholdings are established, 
on said payments, such expenses will be borne by the Sellers, and will be returned to them if 
recovered by the Fund. 
Notwithstanding the above, in the event that current tax legislation should be modified, and 
taxes, charges or withholdings on payments made to the Fund on account of interest of the 
Shares and Certificates are established, which, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, should 
significantly and adversely affect the Fund’s financial balance, termination of the Fund will 
take place, prior liquidation of any remaining assets. In accordance with the provisions of 
section III.10 of the present Prospectus, in which case the Sellers will be able to exercise their 
right of first refusal in accordance with the provisions of this section. 
b) 
The Fund 
Fondos de Titulización de Activos are subject to the general regulations of the Impuesto sobre 
Sociedades. Incorporation thereof is exempt under the heading Operaciones Societarias of the 
Impuesto sobre Transmisiones Patrimoniales y Actos Jurídicos Documentados in accordance 
with article 5º.10 of Law 19/1992. Royal Decree 926/1998, sets forth that the rule provided 
under Law 19/1992 shall apply to Fondos de Titulización de Activos.  
c) 
Sociedad Gestora  
Services rendered to the Fund by the Sociedad Gestora are exempt from Value Added Tax.

awarded to the Securities nor affects the rights of the holders of the Securities. In any event, the

III.8.  Replacement of the Participants 
Financial Agent 
The Sociedad Gestora is entitled to replace the Financial Agent (in all or some of its 
maintenance duties of the Collection Account, Treasury Account, Payment Agency or 
depository of the Shares and Certificates); provided that this conforms with applicable law, and 
that authorisation of the relevant authorities is given, if necessary. The reason for the 
replacement must be serious and present serious prejudice to the interests of the holders of the 
Securities. Notice will be given regarding the replacement to the CNMV, the Rating Agency 
and the Sellers. 
In the event that the rating of the Financial Agent awarded by the Rating Agency for short-term 
risk is reduced to a rating below P1 awarded by Moody’s, the Sociedad Gestora, prior notice 
thereof to the Rating Agency, must implement one or more of the options described in section 
V.3.8.1 if this Prospectus: 
Furthermore, the Financial Agent may terminate the Financial Service Agreement, prior notice 
to the Sociedad Gestora at least two months in advance, in accordance with the terms set forth 
in the Financial Service Agreement provided that (i) another entity with similar financial 
characteristics to the Financial Agent and with a credit rating for short term risk at least equal to 
P1 in Moody’s case, or other recognised by the Rating Agency and accepted by the Sociedad 
Gestora, replaces it in the duties of the Financial Service Agreement, (ii) the CNMV and the 
Rating Agency are notified, and (iii) the rating granted to the Securities is not impaired. 
Termination will not take place, except with the authorisation of the Sociedad Gestora, until 
two Business Days after the Payment Date following the notice of termination. 
Sociedad Gestora 
The resignation and replacement of the Sociedad Gestora will be regulated in accordance with 
Royal Decree 926/1998, or current applicable legislation. In any event, the replacement of the 
Sociedad Gestora will take place in accordance with the following procedure, provided that it 
does not infringe applicable legal regulations:  
(i) 
The Sociedad Gestora will resign from its duties whenever it deems necessary and 
shall voluntarily request its replacement, via written notice to the CNMV. Notice of 
the new Sociedad Gestora duly authorised and registered with the special registers of 
the CNMV, will also be sent, wherein the latter shall declare its acceptance of the 
position and request the corresponding authorisation. Resignation of the Sociedad 
Gestora and selection of a new entity as Sociedad Gestora of the Fund must be 
approved by the CNMV. In no event will the Sociedad Gestora resign unless all the 
requirements and requirements for the new sociedad to fully assume its duties. The 
Sociedad Gestora will not resign from its duties if, as a result of its replacement, the 
ratings awarded to the Bonds are reduced. All expenses generated as a consequence 
of said replacement will be borne by the Sociedad Gestora itself.

(ii) 
If the Sociedad Gestora should incur in any of the causes set forth in article 260 (1) 
of Ley de Sociedades Anónimas occur, the Sociedad Gestora will be replaced. The 
Sociedad Gestora will notify the CNMV and the Rating Agency of the occurrence of 
any of said causes. In this event, the Sociedad Gestora will be obliged to comply with 
section (i) above, prior to its dissolution. 
(iii) 
In the event that the Sociedad Gestora is declared subject to bankruptcy proceedings 
or if its authorisation should be cancelled, it will appoint a Sociedad Gestora to 
replace it. The replacement will take place before two months have elapsed since the 
date in which the event that determined the replacement took place. If the Sociedad 
Gestora does not find another Sociedad Gestora to take over the administration and 
representation of the Fund, or the CNMV does not authorise the replacement, the 
Fund will be liquidated and the Bonds redeemed, four months after the occurrence of 
the incident which determined the replacement. 
(iv) 
The replacement of the Sociedad Gestora and the selection of a new sociedad, 
approved by the CNMV in accordance with the preceding paragraphs, must be 
accepted by the Rating Agency, and the Daily Bulletin of the AIAF Market. The 
Sociedad Gestora undertakes to grant all the public and private documents necessary 
to proceed with its replacement by another Sociedad Gestora in accordance with the 
requirements of the preceding paragraphs. The replacing Sociedad Gestora will be 
subrogated to the Sociedad Gestora in respect of any rights and obligations 
corresponding thereto. Furthermore, the Sociedad Gestora must forward to the new 
Sociedad Gestora all the documents and accounting and computing reports relating to 
the Fund in its possession. 
Other participants 
In the event of breach of their contractual obligations or in the event of adoption of a corporate 
legal or court resolution for the liquidation, dissolution or receivership of any of the participants 
of this securitisation transaction, or if any of them should request declaration of suspension of 
payments or bankruptcy, or in the vent of admission of a third party request in this regard, the 
Sociedad Gestora may terminate the relevant agreements binding them to the Fund, provided 
that such termination is permitted under applicable law. After termination of the Agreement 
and in the event that it is permitted under applicable law, the new participant shall be 
appointed, if applicable, by the Sociedad Gestora, after consulting the competent administrative 
authorities, so that the rating awarded to the Securities issued by the Fund by the Rating 
Agency is not impaired, and such appointment shall be communicated to the Rating Agency 
and to the CNMV. Replacement of the Sellers as administrators of the mortgage loans is set 
forth ins section IV.2.4 of this Prospectus. Furthermore, replacement of Bear Stearns Bank plc 
as counterparty in the Derivatives Contracts are set forth in section V.3.9 of this Prospectus. 
III.9.  Subcontracting of Participants 
The entities taking part in the securitisation transaction TDA 22-MIXTO, pursuant to their 
corresponding agreements, are entitled to subcontract or delegate to third parties of recognised 
solvency and capacity, the performance of any of the services undertaken, provided it is legally 
possible and (i) with the prior written consent of the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, 
with the Rating Agency’s express acceptance, (ii) the sub-contractor or delegate has a rating 
equal to or greater than the rating required by the Rating Agency, and provided that (iii) the

III.10.  Early Liquidation and Termination of the Fund 
Pursuant to the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund and this Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora is 
entitled to proceed to the early liquidation of the Fund TDA 22-MIXTO when the Outstanding 
Nominal Balance of the Shares and Certificates is less than 10% of the initial balance, provided 
that the proceeds from the liquidation of the assets and the balance at the time of the Accounts 
of the Fund are sufficient to discharge the outstanding obligations to the holders of the 
Securities, in accordance with the priority order of payments described in section V.4. of this 
Prospectus, and provided that all the necessary authorisations have been obtained from the 
relevant authorities.  
The Fund will be terminated only in the following circumstances, and the CNMV and the 
Rating Agency will be informed of such circumstances: 
(i) 
When, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, exceptional circumstances occur 
which render impossible, or extremely difficult, the survival of the financial balance 
of the Fund. In this case, the Sociedad Gestora, after notifying the CNMV, will 
proceed to liquidate the Fund in accordance with the Payment Ranking Order set 
forth in section V.4.2. of this Prospectus. 
(ii) 
In the event set forth in Article 19 of Royal Decree 926/1998, setting forth the 
obligation to perform early liquidation of the Fund in the event that four months after 
an event that justifies the replacement of the Sociedad Gestora, pursuant to 
insolvency proceedings or bankruptcy, no alternative Sociedad Gestora has been 
found to manage the Fund. 
(iii) 
In the event that a failure to pay indicating a serious and permanent imbalance in 
respect of any of the issued Securities takes place, or is expected. In this event, the 
Sociedad Gestora, after notifying the CNMV, will proceed to liquidate the Fund in 
accordance with the rules described in section V.4.2. of this Prospectus. 
(iv) 
In the event of an amendment in tax regulations, in accordance with the provisions of 
section III.6 of this Prospectus, which, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, 
significantly and adversely affects the financial balance of the Fund. 
In any event, the Fund shall be terminated in the event of occurrence of any of the following 
circumstances: 
(i) 
When the Shares and Certificates are totally redeemed. In the event that all the Shares 
and Certificates should have matured and there remain outstanding amounts to be 
collected and paid to the Bond holders, the Fund will be terminated on the Payment

market value, the Sociedad Gestora may request the valuation reports it considers 
necessary. 
The Sociedad Gestora, after making a reserve for termination expenses, will immediately apply

Prospectus. 
In the event that the amount remaining is not a liquid amount and corresponds to the Shares or 
Certificates pending the resolution of legal or notarial proceedings initiated as a consequence of 
non-payment by the Debtor of the Share or Certificate, both the continuation thereof and the 
product of its resolution will correspond to the relevant Sellers.

CHAPTER IV 
INFORMATION RELATING TO THE ASSETS SECURITISED IN

IV.1.  Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates Included in the Fund 
A. Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates. Conditions of Issue 
The Shares and Certificates will be issued by the Sellers and subscribed by the Sociedad 
Gestora on behalf of the Fund TDA 22-MIXTO, by virtue of the Deed of Incorporation of the 
Fund. The Shares and Certificates included in the Fund are represented in the form of seven (7) 
Multiple Deeds. Three (3) Multiple Deeds, issued by Caja Granada, Credifimo and Caixa 
Tarragona representing the whole of the Mortgage Shares issued by each of them, and four (4) 
Multiple Deeds, respectively issued by Caja Granada, Credifimo, Caja Navarra and Caixa 
Terrassa, representing all of the Mortgage Transfer Certificates issued by each of them. The 
Shares and Certificates are issued for a total nominal amount of approximately 530,000,000 
Euro. Each Share and Certificate participates in 100% of the unredeemed principal of each one 
of the Mortgage Loans, and shall accrue an interest rate equal to the nominal interest rate 
accrued from time to time by the corresponding Mortgage Loan. 
The full and unconditional assignment to the Fund of the credit rights derived from the 
Mortgage Loans, by the issue of the Shares and Certificates shall be made as of the 
Disbursement Date for the period remaining until maturity of said loans, without any 
agreement to repurchase on the part of the Sellers. The Shares and Certificates shall not begin 
to accrue the interest mentioned in the foregoing paragraph until the Disbursement Date 
(included), i.e., until December 1, 2004, so that interest accrued by the Mortgage Loans until 
the Disbursement Date shall continue to belong to the relevant Seller, irrespective of the 
accrual period taken into account for the purpose of interest calculation in the Mortgage Loans. 
The Sellers do not assume any liability whatsoever for the non-payment by the mortgage 
debtors of principal, interest or any other amount that may be due under the Mortgage Loans. 
The Sellers do not, under any circumstances, assume any responsibility in guaranteeing, either 
directly or indirectly, the success of the transaction, nor will they give guarantees or warranties, 
nor enter into repurchase agreements for the Shares and Certificates or under the Deed of 
Incorporation of the Fund, the present Issue Prospectus or any other agreement or contract. 
B. Composition of the portfolio 
The assets of TDA 22-MIXTO shall be composed of Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer 
Certificates issued by Caja Granada, Credifimo, Caixa Tarragona, Caja Navarra and Caixa 
Terrassa on loans granted for the acquisition, construction or restoration of housing located 
within Spanish territory, with first mortgage security on a property valued by a Appraisal 
Company. Some of the aforementioned loans originate from debtor replacements in contractor 
loans.

C. Subscription of the Mortgage Shares and the Mortgage Transfer Certificates 
Price, Subscription and Payment of the Shares and Certificates: the Sociedad Gestora shall 
subscribe 100% of the Shares and Certificates on behalf of the Fund. 
The price of the Shares and Certificates will be the nominal amount thereof, and will be paid by 
the Sociedad Gestora, in the name of the Fund, to the Sellers on the Disbursement Date, 
December 9, 2004. 
In the case of resolving the Constitución of the Fund, and consequently, the issue and 
subscription of the Zares and Certificates, (i) the obligation of payment will terminate for the 
Shares and Certificates on the Fund behalf, (ii) the Sociedad Gestora  will have to return to the 
Sellers any right that could have arisen from the fund by the suscription of the Shares and 
Certificates and, (iii) Mortgage Loans will be included on the Asset of the Treasury Account. 
Rights of the Fund derived from the Subscription of Shares and Certificates: The Fund, as 
holder of the Shares and Certificates, shall have the rights recognised in the applicable 
legislation and in the Shares and Certificates. In particular, it will have the right to receive 
payments made by the Mortgage Loan debtors from the Disbursement Date onwards, with the 
exceptions provided in the following paragraph, and any other payment arising from the 
Mortgage Loans, provided such payments correspond to the Shares and Certificates. The 
Shares and Certificates will begin to accrue interest from the Disbursement Date. 
In addition to the payments made by the Mortgage Loan debtors, any other payment received 
by the Sellers in relation to the Mortgage Loans, including those arising from any accessories to 
the Loans such as compensation derived from insurance policies, payments made by possible 
guarantors, etc., will correspond to the Fund, with the exception of delinquent interest, fees for 
unpaid receipt claims, subrogation fees and early cancellation/redemption fees, together with 
any other fee which will correspond to the Sellers of the Shares and Certificates. Additionally, 
the Fund will be entitled to receive amounts, goods or rights in payment of principal or interest 
in the Mortgage Loans, both for the auction price or amount determined by court resolution or 
notarial proceedings in the enforcement of mortgage guarantees, for the disposal or exploitation 
of the properties awarded or as a result of the aforementioned enforcements, in the interim 
administration and possession of the properties subject to enforcement proceedings. The Sellers 
undertake to give the necessary notices so that payments to the Sociedad Gestora may be 
performed. The Sellers must make reasonable efforts to maintain in force and fully effective 
any insurance policies subscribed in relation to the Mortgage Loans, and they will be liable for 
any damages to the Fund in the event the insurance policies have not been maintained.

Notices 
The Sellers will continue to administer the Mortgage Loans in accordance with section IV.2. of 
this Prospectus. The Sociedad Gestora and the Sellers have agreed not to notify the assignment 
to the debtors of the Mortgage Loans as this notice is not a condition for the effectiveness of the 
Issue. 
Pursuant to article 1,527 of the Civil Code, the debtor who pays the creditor before it aware of 
the assignment shall be released from its obligation. The Seller must notify the assignment to 
the relevant Debtors when it is necessary or required in the conditions of the corresponding 
Mortgage Loan, and the Sociedad Gestora so requires it. Following notice, the Debtors will be 
freed of their obligations following payment to the Financial Agent. In accordance with article 
1,198 of the Civil Code, the Debtor that agrees to the assignment will not have recourse against 
the Fund for the compensation due from the Seller. 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, the Sellers will grant the broadest faculties legally required to 
the Sociedad Gestora so that it can notify the assignment to the debtors of the Mortgage Loans 
when it deems necessary. In particular, the Sociedad Gestora will notify the assignment to the 
debtors of the Mortgage Loans in the event of the replacement of the Sellers in the 
administration of the Mortgage Loans and in the event of administrative or judicial 
administration of the Sellers. 
The Sellers will bear the expenses of the notice to the debtors of the Mortgage Loans even if 
the Sociedad Gestora performs such notice. 
D. Replacement of the Mortgage Shares and the Mortgage Transfer Certificates 
In the event that, despite the declarations made by the Sellers and their efforts to ensure 
performance, a particular Mortgage Loan, during the term of the Fund, , suffered from hidden 
defects, including the defect of not complying on the Incorporation Date of the Fund with the 
representations set out in section IV.4. below and set forth in Clause 8.3 of the Deed of 
Incorporation of the Fund, the Sellers undertake: 
(A) 
To replace the corresponding Share and/or Certificate by another one with similar 
financial characteristics in terms of amount, term to maturity and interest rate, and which is 
acceptable to the Sociedad Gestora, prior consultation with the Rating Agency, and provided 
that this does not impair the rating of the Bonds awarded thereby. 
In any case, in the event of replacement of a Share and/or Certificate, the Sellers must 
demonstrate that the Share and/or Certificate is in accordance with the conditions referred to in 
section IV.4. of this Prospectus. 
Each Seller, as soon as it becomes aware that a Share and/or Certificate issued does not 
correspond with the aforementioned representations, will inform the Sociedad Gestora and 
indicate the Mortgage Loans that will be presented to replace the faulty ones. In the event that 
any of the Shares and/or Certificates are replaced in accordance with these provisions, the 
Sellers will issue a new Multiple Deed, which will be exchanged with the one provided in 
accordance with the Deed of Incorporation.

IV.2.  Servicing of the Mortgage Loans 
In accordance with article 61 (3) of Royal Decree 685/1982, of March 17th, and in section 2.b) 
of Article 2 of Royal Decree 926/1998, each Seller undertakes in the Deed of Incorporation of 
the Fund, to maintain the custody and servicing of the Mortgage Loans serving as backing for 
the Shares and Certificates are derived, remaining responsible to undertake whatever actions 
are necessary for the effective collection of the Mortgage Loans. In any case, the Sociedad 
Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will undertake to exercise all powers that, in the case of default 
in the payment by the borrower, correspond to the holders of Shares and Certificates in article 
66 of Royal Decree 685/1982.  
All taxes, direct or indirect, charges or expenses accrued and incurred by the Sellers or those 
that must pass on in relation to the evolution of the services of the administration of the 
Mortgage Loans, without prejudice to its right to receive reimbursement from the debtors or 
from the Fund in the event of their recovery.

General Commitments of the Seller as Administrator 
Each Seller, in relation to the Loans it administers, will declare to the Sociedad Gestora and the 
Fund in the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund that it will:

IV.2.2. 
Administration of the Mortgage Loans 
In the administration of the Mortgage Loans, each Seller will dedicate the same amount and 
attention and will exert the same level of ability, detail and diligence in said administration, 
as would employ in the administration of mortgage loans not assigned, and in any event, 
will exercise a reasonable level of ability, detail and diligence when undertaking its services. 
Each Seller, as Mortgage Loan Administrator shall be subject to the criteria set forth for the 
administration thereof in Appendix 7 to the Deed of Incorporation, although it may modify 
such criteria, provided that said modifications do not imply an impairment of the 
administration of the Mortgage Loans, and the Sociedad Gestora is notified, and the rating 
granted to the Bonds by the Rating Agency is not affected.

Specifically, each Seller, in respect of Mortgage Loan administered thereby, will keep under 
safe custody all the deeds, documents, files and any other ancillary rights of the Mortgage 
Loans, together with any relevant documents, and shall not relinquish possession, custody or 
control thereof, unless there is prior written consent from the Sociedad Gestora, in the name 
of the Fund, unless it is (i) in favour of a sub-contracted or delegated party in accordance 
with applicable law; or (ii) to allow the Seller, as Loan Administrator, to bring legal action 
for the enforcement of a Mortgage Loan. 
Each Seller, as loan administrator, will continue to collect all the amounts due and payable, 
by virtue of the Mortgage Loans or any accessory right thereto, and will make its best effort 
so as to ensure that all payments to be made by the debtors or by any other person, by virtue 
of the Mortgage Loans or any accessory right thereto, are collected, in accordance with the 
terms and conditions of the referred Mortgage Loans, on the corresponding dates. 
a) Recourse against the Debtors 
In the event of delay in the payments from the debtors of the shared Mortgage Loans, each 
Seller, as Loan Administrator, shall take the usual steps to remedy such situation, described 
in Appendix 7 of the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund, adopting the actions available to a 
reasonably prudent creditor undertaking financial operations in Spain, provided that the 
exercise of said faculties do not affect the management of the Fund, nor the rating of the 
Bonds. 
In any event, and for the event of non-payment by the debtor of the Mortgage loans serving 
as backing for the issue of Shares and Certificates included in the Fund, the Sociedad 
Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will undertake the exercise of all the faculties set forth in 
Article 66 of Royal Decree 685/1982. 
In the event of section b) of article 66 of Royal Decree 685/1982, the right of adjudication 
will correspond to the Seller and the distribution of the price will be effected as set forth in 
said article. 
In the event that any of the circumstances described in sections c) and d) of article 66 of 
Royal Decree 685/1982 take place, and as a consequence, the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf 
of the Fund, is subrogated to the position of the Seller in the procedure initiated by the 
Seller, or initiates a process of foreclosure, the Sociedad Gestora will sell the affected 
properties in the shortest possible time under market conditions. The relevant Seller will 
have the right to repurchase the properties mortgaged as guarantee of the Loans it 
administers, during the 10 business days from the date in which the Sociedad Gestora 
notifies the intention to sell the property. The right to repurchase will imply that the Seller 
will be able to purchase the properties in the same conditions it was offered to the Sociedad 
Gestora. 
All the options outlined in this section in relation to the Shares and Certificates will be 
carried out in the terms set forth in Title IV of Book III of Law 1/2000 de Enjuiciamiento 
Civil.

b) Recourse against the Sellers 
The Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will be entitled to exercise enforcement actions

the procedures set forth in the Ley de Enjuiciamiento Civil. 
Following the termination of the Mortgage Loans, the Fund, through the Sociedad Gestora, will 
maintain the right to take action against the Sellers until all its obligations have been carried 
out. 
IV.2.3. 
Subcontracting 
The Seller, in relation to the Mortgage Loans administered thereby, is entitled to subcontract 
or delegate to third parties of recognised solvency and capacity, the performance of the 
duties mentioned in Clause 10 of the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund , provided it is 
legally admitted under applicable law and (i) with the prior written consent of the Sociedad 
Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, (ii) the sub-contractor or delegate has a rating equal or 
higher than the rating required by the Rating Agency, and provided that (iii) the 
subcontractor or delegate has waived all rights of recourse against the Fund. 
In any event, neither the Sociedad Gestora nor the Fund Shall assume any liability other 
than as assumed hereunder, in respect of any costs or expenses payable or incurred as a 
result of the subcontracting or delegation or derived from the termination of any Agreement 
in this regard.  
Notwithstanding a subcontract or delegation, the Seller will not be exonerated nor liberated 
from said subcontract or delegation of any of the responsibilities undertaken by virtue of the 
Deed of Incorporation of the Fund. 
IV.2.4. 
Replacement of the Seller by the Sociedad Gestora as Administrator of the Shares 
and Certificates 
In the event that the Sociedad Gestora verifies the breach, by the Seller, as Mortgage Loan 
administrator, of the obligations set forth in this section, or the occurrence of events that, in 
the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, entail a prejudice or risk to the financial structure of 
the Fund or to the rights and interests of the Bond holders, the Sociedad Gestora will, in 
accordance with applicable law, (i) replace the Seller as administrator of the Shares and 
Certificates or (ii) request the Seller to subcontract or delegate the undertaking of said 
obligations to the person that, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, has the appropriate 
technical capacity to carry out such obligations. The Sociedad Gestora will take into account 
the proposals made by the Seller in the designation of a substitute. The Seller will carry out 
such subcontracting or delegation. 
Furthermore, it a corporate, legal or judicial decision is reached concerning the liquidation, 
dissolution or receivership of the Seller or it requests to be declared subject to legal 
bankruptcy proceedings, or in the event of admission of a request therefor formulated by a

IV.2.5. 
Amendments of the Mortgage Loans 
In accordance with article 25 of Royal Decree 685/1982 of March, 17th, the Seller is not 
entitled (without the consent of the Sociedad Gestora) to voluntarily cancel [them] for any 
other reason other than payment of the Mortgage Loans, to waive or compound them, to 
make a novation of the Mortgage Loans, to remit or pardon them partially or in full, to 
prorogue them or, in general, carry out any act that might impair or decrease the rank, legal 
enforceability or economic value of the Mortgages or the Mortgage Loans except by the 
modifications outlined in the following paragraph. 
The Seller, as administrator of its Mortgage Loans, will, from the Incorporation Date of the 
Fund, be authorised, provided that the rating awarded to the Bonds is not impaired, that 
payments to the Fund are not adversely affected, and that notice is given to the Sociedad 
Gestora and by the latter to the Rating Agency, to: 
 
(i) 
Permit subrogation of the Mortgage Loan agreements, provided that the characteristics 
of the new Borrower are similar to those of the existing Borrower and that these are 
consistent with the criteria contained in the Seller’s Internal Memorandum On the 
Granting of Mortgage Loans. 
(ii) 
Agree with the Mortgage Borrowers modifications in the rate of interest and final 
maturity of the Loans, provided the commitments taken by the Seller by virtue of the 
commitments referred to in this section are in full force. 
Modifications in the Interest Rate: In accordance with the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund 
and in the present Prospectus, in the event that a Seller agrees to modify the interest in a 
Mortgage Loan, and, consequently, of the relevant Share or Certificate, the whole of ordinary 
interest accrued by the Mortgage Loan will continue to correspond to the Fund.

Mortgage Loans 1, and April 30, 2044 for Mortgage Loans 2.  
 
c)

instalments in the six months prior to the modification, and the Mortgage Loan is 
currently up to date in its payments. 
d)

Mortgage Loan is granted and registered with the Registro de la Propiedad while 
preserving, for first rank mortgages, said rank. 
e) 
That expenses derived from the amendment of the Mortgage Loans are borne by the 
corresponding Seller or the loan debtor and, in no event by the Fund. 
f) 
That the amount resulting from the sum of the initial balance of the Shares and 
Certificates with an extended final maturity date does not exceed 5% of the initial 
balance of the Shares and Certificates included in the Fund and corresponding to the 
Seller. 
g) 
In no event will the Seller, in its capacity as administrator of the loans, decide 
without prior request from the mortgage borrower, the modification of the final 
maturity date of the Mortgage Loan. The administrator will act, in relation to said 
modification, always taking into account the interests of the Fund. 
The Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will, at any time during the life of the Fund, 
cancel or suspend the modification of the final maturity date on behalf of the Seller. 
The amendment of the Mortgage Loan will not prevent it from remaining adjusted to the 
representations and warranties included in section IV.4. of this Prospectus.

IV.3.  Mechanisms for Granting the Mortgage Loans 
The Mortgage Loans have been granted by the Sellers for the purpose of financing with a 
Mortgage security the acquisition, construction or restoration of residences located in Spain. A 
first or second rank Mortgage on the full ownership of each and every property guarantees said 
loans in question. 
On the Incorporation Date, as declared by the Sellers, there are no lawsuits of any kind 
whatsoever relating to the Mortgage Loans that could impair their validity. 
The Loans have been granted by the Sellers in accordance with their usual procedures, which 
are described in Appendix 7 of the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund, Memorandum for the 
Granting of Mortgage Loans.

IV.4.  Representations and warranties in respect of the Sellers, the Mortgage Shares and 
Mortgage Transfer Certificates and the Mortgage Loans 
Each of the Sellers, as holder of its Mortgage Loans, shall represent and warrant to the Fund 
and to the Sociedad Gestora, regarding itself, the Shares and Certificates issued thereby and 
regarding the Mortgage Loans serving as backing for the Shares and the Certificates issued 
by each of them that, on the Incorporation Date of the Fund: 
IV.4.1. 
With respect to the Sellers 
1) That they are credit institutions duly incorporated in accordance with applicable law, they 
are registered with the Registro Mercantil and they are authorised to participate in the 
Mortgage Loan Market. 
2) That they have not been declared subject to bankruptcy proceedings as of the date of this 
Prospectus nor at any time since their incorporation. 
3) That they have obtained all of the required authorisations, both administrative and 
corporate, for the valid granting of the Deed of Incorporation and the commitments 
undertaken in such deed and the other agreements relating to the incorporation of the 
Fund. 
4) That they have individual and consolidated annual accounts for the last three financial 
years, with the favourable opinion, without reserves, of their Auditors, at least for the 
previous financial year, although in respect of Caixa Terrassa, the audit reports for 
financial year 2003 present a reserve which is not referred to any circumstance involving 
impairment of its solvency or credit. All of the Entities have filed such annual accounts 
and audit reports with the CNMV and with the Commercial Registry.  
5) They comply with applicable law regarding data protection. 
IV.4.2. 
With respect to the Shares and Certificates 
1) That the Shares and Certificates are issued in accordance with Law 2/1981, Royal Decree 
685/1982 and Additional Provision 5 of Law 3/1994 in the wording set out by article 18 
of Law 44/2002 and other applicable legislation and satisfy all requirements set forth 
therein for the issue of the Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates; and in 
particular that the issue of the Shares satisfies the provisions of articles 59 and 62 of 
Royal Decree 685/1982, with respect to the amount of mortgage warrants issued by the 
relevant Seller. The Mortgage Shares are issued with the protection of the Mortgage 
Loans 1, satisfying all the requirements in Section II of Law 2/1981 and Chapter 2 of

That all Mortgage Loans are fully withdrawn, and are denominated and payable in 
Euro. 
7.

Mortgage security the acquisition, construction or restoration of residences located in 
Spain.

market and council houses, located in Spain. Regarding mortgage loans granted over

in Appendix 4 of the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund and in the Multiple Deeds.

11.

Companies duly registered with the Bank of Spain, and that the appraisals have been 
appropriately certified. Such appraisals fulfil all requirements set forth in legislation 
applicable to the mortgage market, taking into account that, in the case of protected 
council housing, the market appraisal value has been taken as appraisal value of the 
mortgaged residences.

each Mortgage Loan 2, on the date of the issue of the Mortgage Transfer Certificates. 
15. 
That the Sellers are not aware of any reduction of more than 20% of the appraisal 
value of the value of any of the properties. 
16. 
That all properties subject to mortgage have damages insurance, the insured amount 
covering either the appraisal value of the properties (excluding elements which are, 
by nature, uninsurable, i.e. the value of the land), or the outstanding balance of the 
loan on November 9, 2004.

That the information submitted by the Sellers regarding the insurance against 
damages taken by the mortgage debtors and any other ancillary rights relating to the

as far as the Seller is aware. 
18. 
That the Sellers are not aware of any failure to pay in full the insurance premiums 
referred to in paragraphs (16) and (17).

IV.4.3.1. 
Homogeneity of the Loans  
The mortgage loans backing the Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates included 
in the Fund have been granted by Spanish credit entities, with the purpose of financing the 
acquisition, construction and restoration of housing, following the standard market analysis and 
granting criteria. Thus, all Mortgage Loans included in the Fund may be considered 
homogeneous.

V.1.1. Assumptions 
The tables below refer to three of the possible assumptions, (constant prepayment rates of 
5%, 10% and 15%) that, in respect of the income and payments made by the Fund, might 
occur during the life of the Fund and the securities issue. 
For the calculation of the financial service table of the Fund, data have been taken from the 
portfolio referred to in the preceding Chapter IV.3.2 on October 21, 2004.

CHAPTER V –Financial and Economic Information relating to the Fund TDA 22-Mixto 
This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with 
the "Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") November 30, 2004. 
The "Folleto Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto 
Informativo" shall have any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Bond Issue. 
 
Relating to the Shares and Certificates 
• 
Volume of the Loan Portfolio from which the Loans underlying the issue of Mortgage 
Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates will be selected: 582,681,175.59 on 
November 9, 2004. 
Mortgage Shares:  
 
 
 
314,324,681.53.- Euro 
Mortgage Transfer Certificates: 
 
 
268,356,494.06.- Euro 
• 
Maximum amount of Outstanding Nominal Balance that the Shares will represent in the 
Date of Incorporation of the Fund: 286,000,000 Euro. 
• 
Maximum amount of Outstanding Nominal Balance that the Certificates will represent 
in the Date of Incorporation of the Fund: 244,000,000 Euro. 
• 
Interest Rate: the weighted average interest rate for the Mortgage Shares’ portfolio is 
3.72%, and 3.59% for the Mortgage Transfer Certificates, without prejudice to the 
revisions which will be performed in accordance with the following paragraph. 
• 
The interest rate of the Mortgage Loans on each period: the interest rate in force for 
each loan for each period shall be applied. After the month on which the interest rate of 
the Mortgage Loans is to be reviewed for the first time, the margin in force for each 
period shall be applied to each of them over the reference rate in force at the time.  
• 
Weighted average initial life of the Shares contained in the portfolio: 273 months. For 
Certificates it is 347 months. 
• 
Annual early redemption rate: assumption 5%, 10% and 15%. 
• 
An annual percentage of delay without Default of 0% is assumed for Shares and 
Certificates, i.e., the portfolio of Shares and Certificates would not reach the default 
levels provided in sections II.11.2.1 and II.11.2.2., for Shares and sections II.11.3.1 and 
II.11.3.2 for Certificates, so that the financial service tables reflect the application of the 
redemption rules provided in section II.11.2.1 for Shares and section II.11.3.1 for 
Certificates. 
• 
An annual percentage Share Default rate: 0.3% is assumed for Defaulted Mortgage 
Shares, from Dicember 2005, and 75% recoveries from the defaulted stock a year later. 
The same assumption applies to Mortgage Transfer Certificates.

Other Deposited Resources 
The difference between the amount corresponding to the issue of the Securities and the 
balance of the Share and Certificates acquired by the Fund is included under the heading 
“Other Deposited Resources”. This amount, 0.54 Euro in the preceding balance, will be 
deposited at the Treasury Account until the first Payment Date, date in which it will be 
allocated in full to the Bonds’ redemption.

Subordinated Loan 1 
• 
Amount: 1,200,000.- Euro. The amount of the Loan will be used by the Sociedad 
Gestora to cover the difference, on the first Payment Date, between interest accrual and 
payment of the Mortgage Shares. 
• 
Interest Rate: Subordinated Loan 1 bears a floating annual interest rate equal to the 
Reference Interest Rate of the Bonds during such period plus a margin of 0.75%. 
• 
Redemption: Redemption of Loan 1 will take place on each Payment Date by a 
reduction of the outstanding principal in relation to the need for resources to cover the 
difference between the accrual and payment of interest of the Mortgage Shares. 
Subordinated Loan 2 
• 
Amoun: 1,000,000.- Euro. The amount of the Loan will be used by the Sociedad 
Gestora to cover the difference, on the first Payment Date, between accrual and 
payment of interest of the Mortgage Transfer Certificates. 
• 
Interest Rate: Subordinated Loan 2 bears a floating annual interest rate equal to the 
Reference Interest Rate of the Bonds during such period plus a margin of 0.75%. 
• 
Redemption: Redemption of Loan 2 will take place on each Payment Date by a 
reduction of the outstanding principal in relation to the need for resources to cover the 
difference between accrual and payment of interest of the Mortgage Transfer 
Certificates. 
Initial Expenses Loan 1 
• 
Amount: 324,765.56.- Euro. The amount of the Loan will be used pay the initial 
expenses of the Fund corresponding to the Class 1 Bonds. 
• 
Interest Rate: the Loan bears a floating annual interest rate equal to the Reference 
Interest Rate of the Bonds during such period plus a margin of 0.75%. 
• 
Redemption: Redemption of the Initial Expenses Loan will be made in 20 consecutive 
and equal instalments, the first of which will take place on the first Payment Date 
(March 29, 2005) and the rest on the following Payment Dates. 
Initial Expenses Loan 2 
• 
Amount: 307,440.- Euro. The amount of the Loan will be used pay the initial expenses 
of the Fund corresponding to the Class 2 Bonds. 
• 
Interest Rate: the Loan bears a floating annual interest rate equal to the Reference 
Interest Rate of the Bonds during such period plus a margin of 0.75%. 
• 
Redemption: Redemption of the Initial Expenses Loan will be made in 20 consecutive 
and equal instalments, the first of which will take place on the first Payment Date 
(March 29, 2005) and the rest on the following Payment Dates.

Informativo" shall have any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Bond Issue. 
 
Reserve Funds 1 and 2: Provided with the subscription price for Security IO-1 and 
Security IO-2, and Participating Loan 1 and Participating Loan 2. Reduction of Reserve 
Funds 1 and 2 shall be determined by he Minimum Level of Reserve Fund 1 and 2, 
respectively. The amount thereof shall be invested in the Treasury Account of the Fund at a 
rate of EONIA -0.35%. 
Reinvestment of the Flows: The cash flows received by the Fund (principal and interest of 
the Loan portfolios) will be reinvested at an interest rate equal to EONIA -0,35%. 
Fees: Fees for the Sociedad Gestora. On each Payment Date, a fixed fee of 18,750 Euro plus 
1/4 of 0.0320%% of the Outstanding Nominal Balance pending maturity of the Shares and 
Certificates at the beginning of the Collection Period. It is assumed hereunder that there are 
no additional expenses for the Fund. 
V.1.2. 
Table of Income and Expenses of the Fund 
 
IMPORTANT NOTE FOR THE INVESTOR 
The information in the following table is provided for information purposes only, and the amounts 
mentioned therein do not represent particular payment obligations by the Fund to third parties on the 
corresponding dates or periods to which they refer. The data have been calculated under assumptions 
of constant default and prepayment rates throughout the life of the Fund, but which in reality are 
subject to continuous change; therefore, any investor interested in knowing the expected payment 
schedule on any particular date should request the pertinent information from the institution authorised 
to distribute it, the Sociedad Gestora, AIAF market and the CNMV. Notwithstanding the foregoing, 
this information is also available through the Underwriters and others active in the secondary market. 
Furthermore, the interest rate of the Bonds used for purposes of the calculation in the following table 
of the financial service of the Fund might not coincide with the rate awarded on the Disbursement 
Date. The Financial Service Table in Euro is shown for information purposes only, as all payments of 
interest and principal of the Bonds, together with the fee, will be effected, from the Disbursement 
Date, in Euro, currency in which the securities have been issued.

CHAPTER V –Financial and Economic Information relating to the Fund TDA 22-Mixto 
This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with 
the "Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") November 30, 2004. 
The "Folleto Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto 
Informativo" shall have any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Bond Issue. 
 
 
V.1.3. 
Time Schedule of the Fund 
Incorporation Date: December 1, 2004. Incorporation of the Fund, Issue and Subscription by 
the Fund of the Shares and Certificates and issue of the Securities. 
Disbursement Date: December 9, 2004. Disbursement of the Securities and payment of the 
Shares and Certificates. Beginning of the accrual of interest on the Shares and Certificates and 
the Securities issued. 
Calculation Periods of the Sellers: Calendar months. Settlement of amounts collected from 
borrowers shall be made to the Fund according to such monthly periods. 
Collection Dates of the Fund: Transfer by the Sellers, as loan administrators, of their loans to 
the Collection Account. Caja Granada will pay amounts on a daily basis; Credifimo, Caixa 
Tarragona, Caixa Terrassa and Caja Navarra will pay amounts on a weekly basis, every 
Tuesday or, in the event that such date should not be a Business Day, payment will take place 
on the immediately subsequent Business Day. 
Payment Dates of the Fund: March 28, June 28, September 28 and December 28 of every year 
during the life of the Fund. Payment to the holders of the Securities issued, payment of interest 
on the Loans (Initial Expenses Loans 1 and 2 and Subordinated Loans 1 and 2), payment of fees 
to the Sociedad Gestora, and repayment of the principal of the Loans (Initial Expenses Loans 1 
and 2 and Subordinated Loans 1 and 2) and remaining payments of the Fund. In the event that 
such date is not a Business Day, payment will take place on the immediately following 
Business Day. 
Determination Date: The interest rate applicable for each accrual period for all Bond Series will 
be determined on the second Business Day prior to the Payment Date on which begins the 
corresponding accrual period. The first Determination Date will be December 7, 2004, i.e., the 
second Business Day prior to the Disbursement Date. 
Notice Dates: March 26, June 26, September 26 and December 26 of each year for the entire 
life of the Fund. Notice of the amounts to be paid on account of principal and interest to the 
holders of the Bonds. In the event that such date should not be a Business Day, notice will be 
given on the immediately preceding Business Day 
A Business Day shall be any day of the week on which it is possible to perform transactions in 
accordance with the TARGET schedule.   
V.2.  Accounting criteria of the Fund 
The Fund will account for income and expenses on an accrual basis. 
a) Mortgage Shares and Mortgage Transfer Certificates subscribed by the Fund: the Shares and 
Certificates are registered on the balance sheet of the Fund in an amount equal to their nominal 
amount. 
Interest on the Shares and Certificates are registered in the profit and loss account on an accrual 
basis. 
 
115


CHAPTER V –Financial and Economic Information relating to the Fund TDA 22-Mixto 
This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with 
the "Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") November 30, 2004. 
The "Folleto Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto 
Informativo" shall have any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Bond Issue. 
 
Interest due, but unpaid, on the Shares and Certificates not declared Defaulted are registered as an 
asset on the balance sheet. 
Matured interest and outstanding principal of the Shares and Certificates declared Defaulted are 
registered as an asset, except in those cases in which it can be demonstrated that the Mortgaged 
property does not provide a sufficient guarantee. 
b) Bonds issued: The Bonds are registered as a liability on the balance sheet of the Fund, in an 
amount equal to their reimbursement value. 
Interest payable pursuant to the Bonds is registered in the profit and loss account on an accrual 
basis; the portion thereof which has thus accrued which is due, but unpaid, is registered in a related 
liabilities account set forth for such purposes. 
c) Securities IO-1 and Securities IO-2: shall be registered as liabilities of the Fund, for their 
subscription price, adjusted from time to time in all Payments IO-1 and Payments IO-2, 
respectively, performed up to the date in question. 
d) Accounts of the Fund: Liquidity accounts of the Fund held at the Financial Agent, and as the 
case may be, at the Rated Sellers, with pre-established reinvestment mechanisms. 
The amount of the accounts is registered as an asset of the Fund, while the income and expenses of 
this account are part of the income and expenses of the Fund. 
e) Operation expenses, fees and remunerations: All fees and expenses are deductible during their 
accrual period. 
f) Technical Advances: On every Calculation Date, the Technical Advance obtained on the 
preceding Calculation Date is considered as deductible from the payment corresponding to the 
Calculation Period subject to payment, and a new Technical Advance, corresponding to the 
subsequent payment, may be requested. 
g) Initial Expenses Loans 1 and 2, Subordinated Loans 1 and 2 and Participating Loans 1 and 2: 
Interest of these Loans (Initial Expenses Loans 1 and 2,l Subordinated Loans 1 and 2 and 
Participating Loans 1 and 2) will be accounted for in every period on an accrual basis. 
Financial year: The accounting periods of the Fund shall commence on January 1st and end on 
December 31st of each year, except for the first accounting period, which will commence on the 
Incorporation Date and end on December 31st, 2004.  
Result: The net result in each financial year must be nil.

The amount of Subordinated Loan 1 will be delivered on the Business Day prior to the first 
Payment Date, i.e. on March 24, 2005, by payment thereof into the Treasury Account opened in 
the name of the Fund at the Financial Agent. 
This amount of Subordinated Loan 1 will be used by the Sociedad Gestora to cover the difference, 
on the first Payment Date, between the interest of the Mortgage Shares accrued and paid.  
Subordinated Loan 1 will accrue a floating interest rate equal to the Reference Interest Rate of the 
Bonds in force at each moment plus a margin of 0.75%. Payment of said interest shall take place 
on each Payment Date and shall be subject to the priority order described in section V.4.2. for 
Available Resources 1.  
Maturity of Subordinated Loan 1 will take place on the date of the liquidation of the Fund. 
Nevertheless, redemption of Subordinated Loan 1 on each Payment Date will be free until its 
redemption, and the Sociedad Gestora will decide in accordance with the need for estimated 
resources to cover the balance between the accrual and payment of the Mortgage Shares by the 
Securitisation Fund. Distribution of such redemptions between the Lenders 1 shall be made by the 
Sociedad Gestora in accordance with the Contrato de Gestión Interna Individualizada. 
The entirety of the amounts payable to the Sellers, for both interest accrued and redemption of 
principal, accrued by Subordinated Loan 1, will be subject to the priority order set forth in section 
V.4.2. for the Available Resources 1, and, consequently, will only be paid to the Sellers on any 
specific Payment Date, in the event that the Available Resources 1 of the Fund on such Payment 
Date are sufficient to attend the obligations of the Fund listed in sections (i) through (xi) of said 
section in relation to interests and (i) through (xiv) for the principal.  
All amounts, which, with respect to the above sections, are not paid to the Lenders 1 will be 
effected on the following Payment Dates in which the Available Resources 1 allow for such a 
payment in accordance with the established priority order. 
Those amounts owed to the Lenders 1 and not paid pursuant to the provisions of the 
aforementioned sections, will not accrue penalty interest in their favour.

V.3.5. 
Participating Loan 1 
Caixa Tarragona shall grant, in accordance with the provisions of Participating Loan 
Agreement 1, a subordinated loan to the Fund (hereinafter, “Participating Loan 1”) allocated by 
the Sociedad Gestora to the partial funding of Reserve Fund 1. 
The total amount of Participating Loan 1 shall be 1,067,043,88.-Euro. 
The amount of Participating Loan 1 shall be delivered on the Disbursement Date by payment of 
the amount thereof into the Treasury Account. 
Redemption of Participating Loan 1 shall take place, on each Payment Date, proportionally to 
the reduction of Reserve Fund 1 corresponding to Caixa Tarragona, subject to the priority 
payment order provided under section V.4.2. for Available Resources 1 in this Prospectus.  
As a result of the subordinated nature of Participating Loan 1, in respect of the remaining 
obligations of the Fund and to the fact that repayment thereof depends on the results of the 
Mortgage Shares issued by Caixa Tarragona, and on the evolution of interest rates payable to 
Class 1 Securities issued by the Fund, remuneration of the Participating Loan 1 shall have two 
elements, a fixed element and a variable one, relating to the evolution of the risks pertaining to 
the Fund: 
(i) 
“Fixed Remuneration of Participating Loan 1”: the Outstanding Nominal Balance of 
Participating Loan 1 shall accrue interest calculated based on a floating annual interest 
rate equal to the reference interest rate for the Bonds in force from time to time, as 
described under section II.10. of this Prospectus, plus a margin of 1%. 
 
(ii) 
“Variable Remuneration of Participating Loan 1”, which shall be calculated in 
accordance with the provisions of section III.4.3 of this Prospectus.

Reserve Fund 1

The Reserve Fund 1 will be constituted on the Disbursement Date, with charge to the whole of 
Participating Loan 1 for an amount of 1,067,043.88 Euro and also to part of the subscription 
price of Security IO-1, for an amount of 1,935,956.12 Euro. The amount of Reserve Fund 1 has

Caja Granada:

On each Payment Date, the Reserve Fund 1 will be funded, as the case may be, until the 
Minimum Level of the Reserve Fund 1 is reached, with the resources that, on each Payment 
Date, are available for such purpose, in accordance with the priority order described in section 
V.4.2. for Available Resources 1. 
The Minimum Level of the Reserve Fund 1 will be the lesser of the following amounts: 
- 1.05% of the sum of the initial amount of the issue of Class 1 Bonds. 
- 2.10% of the sum of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the issue of the Class 1 Bonds.  
No reduction of the Reserve Fund 1 will be made when one of the following situations takes 
place: 
1) If the amounts allocated to redemption of the Bonds on the current Payment Date are 
less than the amount determined in point (a) of section II.11.2.1. of this Prospectus. 
2) The Outstanding Nominal Balance pending maturity of the Non-Defaulted Shares with 
defaults equal to or greater than 90 days is higher than 1% of the Outstanding Nominal 
Balance pending maturity of the Non-Defaulted Shares. 
3) If the Sociedad Gestora does not decide to liquidate the Fund, when the Outstanding 
Nominal Balance of the Shares and Certificates is below 10% of their initial balance. 
In any event, the Minimum Level of the Reserve Fund 1 will not fall below 0.75% of the initial 
balance of the Class 1 Bonds. 
The amounts of the Reserve Fund 1 will be deposited at the Treasury Account with the 
guarantees described in section V.3.8. of this Prospectus. In the event that the Seller becomes a 
Rated Seller, the proportion of the Reserve Fund 1 it has forwarded, in relation to its share in 
the Participating Loan 1, as set forth by Clause 16 of the Deed of Incorporation of the Fund, 
will be paid to the Reinvestment Account with charge to the Treasury Account on the following 
Payment Date. 
(ii) 
Reserve Fund 2 
As credit enhancement mechanism to cover for possible losses due to unpaid and/or defaulted 
Mortgage Loans 2, and in order to allow the payments to be made by the Fund, in accordance 
with the priority order set forth in section V.4.2. for the Available Resources 2 of this 
Prospectus, a “Reserve Fund 2” will be established, for a total amount of 5,514,400.- Euro, i.e., 
2.26% of the initial amount of the Class 2 Bonds.

V.3.8. 
Deposit of the Resources of the Fund 
V.3.8.1. 
Collection Account 
The Fund will have at the Financial Agent, as set forth in the Financial Service 
Agreement, a bank account in the name of the Fund (“Collection Account”) 
through which on each Collection Date, corresponding to each Seller, all amounts 
due to the Fund from each Seller derived from the loans serviced thereby. 
Amounts deposited with the Collection Account corresponding to the total amount 
collected, derived from the mortgage loans serviced by each Seller during the 
calendar month prior to each Calculation Date (hereinafter, “Collected Amount”) 
shall be paid, together with the relevant Technical Advance, into the Treasury 
Account, prior to 11:30 a.m. of the relevant Calculation Date, with value date on 
the same date. 
The returns of the Collection Account shall be transferred on each Payment Date 
to the Treasury Account. 
The Collection Account may not show a negative balance against the Fund. 
Amounts deposited into the Collection Account will accrue a floating interest rate 
in favour of the Fund, which will be settled on a monthly basis (on the last day of 
each month), based on the floating interest rate resulting from reducing the average 
daily EONIA rates corresponding to the current month by a margin of 0.35%. 
EONIA means the reference rate of the Euro Monetary Market applicable from 
time to time, of the convention in force from time to time, sponsored by the 
European Banking Federation and the Financial Markets Association (currently 
the convention sets forth the reference rate in the Telerate screen, between 18:45 
(Central European Time) and 19:00 (Central European Time) for financings with 
delivery of Funds on the Business Day on which the relevant Interest Period

In the event that the rating of the Financial Agent, given by the Rating Agency for 
short term risk, is reduced below P1, for Moody’s, the Sociedad Gestora will, prior 
consultation with the Rating Agency, take one of the following decisions within 
the 30 days following said downgrading. The Sociedad Gestora will, take 
necessary options to maintain an adequate level of guarantee in respect of the 
commitments derived from the maintenance of the Collection Account: 
1. Obtain from a credit entity with rating for short term risk no less than P1, 
granted by Moody’s, or other recognised by the Rating Agency, a 
guarantee regarding the commitments assumed by the Financial Agent. 
2. Replace the Financial Agent for another credit entity with a rating no less 
than P1, granted by Moody’s, or other recognised by the Rating Agency, 
that will assume, under the same conditions, the functions of the Financial 
Agent. 
V.3.8.2. 
Treasury Account 
The Fund will have at the Financial Agent, and as set forth in the Financial Service 
Agreement, a bank account in the name of the Fund (Treasury Account) through 
which on each Calculation Date, the Fund will transfer to the Treasury Account all 
amounts to be received by the Fund from the Sellers from the Collection Account, 
in accordance with the provisions of the foregoing paragraph and the Deed of 
Incorporation. 
Allocations to Reserve Funds 1 and 2, and net amounts of Derivatives Contracts in 
favour of the Fund shall also be paid into the Treasury Account. In the event that, 
in accordance with the provisions of the present Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora 
should proceed to open the Reinvestment Account(s) at the Rated Seller(s), 
allocations to Reserve Funds 1 and 2 shall be paid into such Reinvestment 
Account(s). 
Following instructions by the Sociedad Gestora, all necessary payments to satisfy 
the obligations of the Fund will be made through the Treasury Account. 
The Treasury Account may not have a negative balance against the Fund.  
Amounts deposited into the Treasury Account will accrue a floating interest rate in 
favour of the Fund, which will be settled on a monthly basis (on the last day of 
each month), based on the floating interest rate resulting from reducing the average 
daily EONIA rates corresponding to the current month by a margin of 0.35%, 
according to the definition of EONIA set forth in the foregoing section. 
In the event that the rating of the Financial Agent, given by the Rating Agency 
were reduced, the Sociedad Gestora will take the same action as described in the 
foregoing section. 
V.3.8.3. 
Reinvestment Accounts 
In the event that any Seller obtains a rating equal to the highest rating for short 
term risk, granted by the Rating Agency or any other Rating Agency accepted 
thereby, the Sociedad Gestora, duly informing the CNMV, will open an account in 
the name of the Fund at the corresponding Seller (hereinafter, “Rated Seller”)

Seller will sign a contract with the Sociedad Gestora, the latter acting in the name

from a credit entity with a rating equal to the maximum granted by the Rating 
Agency for short term risk, guaranteeing the total availability of the amounts 
deposited in the Reinvestment Account, the Seller will be able to maintain the 
Reinvestment Account, provided that the rating of the Securities issued by the 
Fund granted by the Rating Agency is not impaired 
At the time of the signing of the Deed of Incorporation, no Seller has a sufficient 
rating, in accordance with this section, to open a Reinvestment Account. 
V.3.9. 
Technical Advance 
Taking into account that some of the delays in the payments made by the borrowers have an 
interim or technical nature, and in order to prevent such delays from negatively affecting the 
flow of payments to the holders of the issued Securities, and taking into account that there is a 
lapse of 20 days between the end of the Collection Period and the Collection Date on behalf of 
the Fund, and that the amounts collected by the Seller, as loan administrator, belong to the 
Fund, the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will be entitled to receive on every 
Calculation Date, acting in the name and on behalf of the Fund, a settlement advance on 
account of such amounts.

The amount of the Technical Advance cannot exceed the amount collected by each Seller, of 
the Loans it administers, for any item related to the Fund in relation to the Shares and 
Certificates, from the end of the last Collection Period until the Calculation Date on which the 
Technical Advance is requested. 
The Sociedad Gestora will calculate the Technical Advance, as an amount equal to the sum of 
the matured amounts and not yet collected by each Seller, during the preceding Calculation 
Period, for principal and interest from the Shares and Certificates issued by each Seller 
underlying the defaulted Mortgage Loans on the Calculation Date on which the Technical 
Advance is requested, taking into account the limitations described in the preceding paragraph. 
The Technical Advance will not exceed, in respect of each Mortgage Loan, to the interests and 
principal on the last instalment. 
On each Calculation Date, the Technical Advance delivered on the preceding Calculation Date 
may be deducted in the settlement of the Calculation Period subject to such settlement,, and a 
new Technical Advance corresponding to the following payment may be requested. 
V.3.10. 
Derivatives Contracts 
In order to mitigate, on the one hand, the base interest rate risk between the assets (Shares and 
Certificates) and the liabilities (Bonds) of the Fund, and, on the other hand, the existing interest 
rate risk as a result of maximum and minimum interest rates set for a certain percentage of Caja 
Caminos’ mortgage loans, the Sociedad Gestora shall execute, in the name and on behalf of the 
Fund, the following agreements: 
1- Derivatives Contract 1 (annual) 
2- Derivatives Contract 1 (biannual) 
3- Derivatives Contract 2 (annual) 
4- Derivatives Contract 2 (biannual) 
Derivatives Contracts shall be executed over 82.52% of the Shares and 100% of the Certificates 
grouped in the Fund. 
The most relevant terms of these contracts are described below: 
In each Derivatives Contract a Swap and a Collar shall be regulated (Cap and Floor). 
Derivatives Contracts 1 (annual) and 2 (annual), shall be established over the percentage of 
Shares and Certificates, respectively, with an annual period for each interest rate revision. 
Derivatives Contracts 1 (biannual) and 2 (biannual), are established over the percentage of 
Shares and Certificates with a biannual period between each interest rate revision.. 
Party A : Bear Stearns Bank Plc 
Party B : The Sociedad Gestora, in the name and on behalf of the Fund. 
Settlement Dates: Settlement dates shall be the same as the Payment Dates of the Bonds, i.e., 
March 28, June 28, September 28 and December 28 or, in the event that said date should not be 
a Business Day, the immediately following Business Day. The first Settlement Date shall be 
March 29, 2005. 
Settlement Periods: Settlement periods shall be the days effectively elapsed between two 
consecutive Settlement Dates, including the first and excluding the last. Exceptionally, the first
