1.-Contrato de Derivado 1 (anual) 
Notional Amount of Derivatives Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Swap: shall be the 
Outstanding Nominal Balance of Class 1 Bonds, in the proportion represented by the 
Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Shares corresponding to Caja Granada and Credifimo, 
with annual interest rate revision, in respect of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Shares 
included in the Fund with annual interest rate revision, on the relevant settlement date. 
Notional Amount of Derivatives Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Cap/Floor: shall be 
the product of the proportion represented by the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Shares 
with annual interest rate revision, of each one of the different Cap/Floor levels set forth in the 
contract over all the Shares with annual interest rate review subject to a Cap and/or Floor on the 
relevant settlement date, in respect of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Shares included 
in the Fund with annual interest rate revision. 
Calculation Factor 1, for the Swap: shall be the average 12 month- EURIBOR rates obtained 
on each of the twelve preceding Reference Dates prior to the start of the current settlement 
period, weighted by the percentage of Shares corresponding to Caja Granada and Credifimo, 
which review their interest rate on each month of the year . 
Calculation Factor 1, for the Cap: shall be the average 12 month- EURIBOR rates obtained 
in each of the twelve preceding Reference Dates prior to the start of the current settlement 
period, weighted by the percentage of Shares corresponding to Caja Granada and Credifimo, 
with a Cap.  
Calculation Factor 1, for the Floor: shall be the average 12 month- EURIBOR rates obtained 
in each of the twelve preceding Reference Dates prior to the start of the current settlement 
period, weighted by the percentage of Shares corresponding to Caja Granada and Credifimo, 
with a Floor.  
Reference Dates: shall be the 26th day of each month, starting on December 26, 2003. 
Amounts payable by Party A pursuant to the Swap: The result of multiplying the “Notional 
Amount of Derivatives Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Swap” times the Reference Interest 
Rate of the Bonds set forth for each Payment Date, as defined in section II.10.1 of the present 
Prospectus; plus a margin of 0.01%. Party A’s part shall be calculated by days effectively 
elapsed based on a 360-day year. 
Amount payable by Party B pursuant to the Swap: shall be the result of multiplying, based 
on days effectively elapsed and on a 360-day year, the “Notional Amount of Derivatives 
Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Swap” times “Calculation Factor 1, for the Swap”. 
Amounts payable by Party A pursuant to the Cap: The result of multiplying the “Notional 
Amount of Derivatives Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Cap/Floor” times “Calculation 
Factor 1 for the Cap/Floor”. Party A’s part shall be calculated by days effectively elapsed based 
on a 360-day year.  
Amount payable by Party B pursuant to the Floor: The amount payable by Party B shall be 
the result of multiplying, based on days effectively elapsed and on a 360-day year, the 
“Notional Amount of Derivatives Contract 1 (annual), pursuant to the Cap/Floor” times 
“Calculation Factor 1, for the Floor”.

V.3.10.1. 
Events of Default Common to all Derivatives Contracts 
If on a Settlement Date the Fund should not pay the amount due to be paid to Bear 
Stearns Bank Plc, pursuant to any of the Derivatives Contracts, the relevant 
Derivatives Contract may be terminated at the request of Bear Stearns Bank Plc. 
In the event that a settlement amount should be payable, the Fund shall assume, if 
applicable, the obligation to pay the settlement amount provided in the terms of 
the relevant Derivatives Contract, all of which in accordance with the Ordinary 
Rules of Priority, described in section V.4.2. of this Prospectus.  
If on a Settlement Date Bear Stearns Bank Plc should not meet its payment 
obligations for the whole amount payable to the Fund pursuant to any of the 
Derivatives Contracts, the Sociedad Gestora may choose to terminate the relevant 
Derivatives Contract. In such case, Bear Stearns Bank Plc shall assume the 
obligation to pay the settlement amount provided in the terms of the relevant 
Derivatives Contract. Furthermore, in such case, if the settlement amount thereof 
were payable by Bear Stearns Bank Plc, and not by the Fund, payment thereof 
shall be made in accordance with the Ordinary Rules of Priority described in 
section V.4.2. of this Prospectus. 
Without prejudice to the provisions of the two foregoing paragraphs, the Sociedad 
Gestora, save in the event of a permanent alteration of the Fund’s financial 
balance, in the name and on behalf of the Fund, shall attempt always to hold a 
derivatives contract in force. 
The settlement amount of the Derivatives Contracts shall be calculated by Bear 
Stearns Bank Plc, as calculation agent the Derivatives Contracts, based on the 
market value of said Contracts. 
V.3.10.2. 
Changes in the rating of Party A  
1.- In the event that Moody’s (i) should reduce the rating of Party A’s unsecured 
unsubordinated long-term obligations below A1 and of Party A’s Guarantor (Bear 
Stearns Companies Inc. or any entity which should replace it), below A2 or (ii) 
should reduce the rating of Party A’s unsecured unsubordinated short-term 
obligations below P-1 (hereinafter, “Moody’s Initial Rating Event”) and of Party 
A’s Guarantor, or any Entity which should replace it, below A2, Party A shall 
proceed as soon as reasonably possible after the aforementioned Moody’s Initial 
Rating Event, at its expense and making reasonable efforts, either: 
(i) 
to transfer all its rights and obligations relating both to Derivatives 
Contracts 1 and 2 (annual) and Derivatives Contracts 1 and 2 
(biannual), to a third party replacement holding the required ratings 
(A2 for long term debt and P-1 for short term debt) with registered 
offices within the same jurisdiction as Party A or Party B;  
(ii)

V.3.10.3. 
Termination of Derivatives Contracts 
The Derivatives Contracts shall be terminated by operation of law in the event that 
the Rating Agency should fail to confirm, prior to the start of the Subscription 
Period, as final, the rating awarded provisionally to each of the Securities. 
The occurrence, as the case may be, of an early termination of Derivatives 
Contracts shall not in itself constitute a cause for early termination of the Fund or 
Early Liquidation thereof, save if, in conjunction with other events or 
circumstances relating to the Fund’s net asset situation, there should be a material 
or permanent alteration in the financial balance thereof. 
Expiration of the Derivatives Contracts shall take place on the liquidation date of 
the Fund.

V.4.1. 
On the Incorporation Date of the Fund and Issue of the Bonds 
1.  
Origin: 
On the Disbursement Date, the Fund will have funds available arising from: 
a) Funds received as a consequence of the issue and placement of the Bonds. 
b) Funds received on account of the Initial Expenses Loans 1 and 2. The Funds on 
account of the Subordinated Loans 1 and 2 will be disbursed on the Business Day 
immediately prior to the first Payment Date of the Fund. 
c) Funds received on account of the Participating Loans 1 and 2. 
2. 
Allocation: 
On the Disbursement Date the Fund will apply the above-mentioned funds to the 
following payments: 
a) Payments on account of the purchase of the Shares and Certificates included in 
the Fund. 
b) Payment of the initial expenses of the fund, in accordance with section III.4.3. of 
this Prospectus. 
c) Constitution of the Reserve Funds 1 and 2.

1. Origin 
The funds available to the Fund on every Payment Date, which are intended for distribution to 
the Bond holders and for payment of the corresponding fees, arise from: 
a) Amounts from the Shares and Certificates on account of principal and current interests. 
b) Amount of the Technical Advance requested from the Sellers and not reimbursed. 
c) Net amount derived from Derivatives Contracts 1 and 2 (annual) and Derivatives Contracts 
1 and 2 (biannual), payable by Party A and, in the event of settlement of Derivatives 
Contracts 1 and 2 (annual) and Derivatives Contracts 1 and 2 (biannual), resulting 
settlement payment in favour of the Fund. 
d) Income from the Accounts of the Fund. 
e) If applicable, other amounts received from the borrowers for reasons other than principal 
and current interest on the Mortgaged Loans.  
f) If applicable, the result of the liquidation of the assets of the Fund. 
2. Allocation: 
In general, the amounts received by the Fund from the Shares and Certificates will be applied 
on each Payment Date to the following concepts, with the following order of priority in the 
event of insufficient funds: 
Ordinary Rules of Priority for the Allocation of the Available Resources 1 
The Available Resources 1 of the Fund, as defined in section III.4.4. of this Prospectus will be 
applied, on each Payment Date, to the following payments, in the following priority order: 
(i) 
Expenses and taxes 
Expenses (save for the fee of the Sociedad Gestora, the Remuneration for Financial 
Intermediation 1 and Floating Remuneration of Participating Loan 1), and extraordinary 
expenses, the latter being understood as such expenses not provided for under section 
III.4.3, together with taxes to be borne by the Fund. All in the same existing proportion, 
at the beginning of the immediately prior Interest Accrual Period, between the Shares 
and all the Shares and Certificates included in the Fund, together with the extraordinary 
expenses originated from the interests of the holders of A1a, A1b, B1, C1 and D1 Bonds. 
(ii) 
Management Fee of the Sociedad Gestora 
Remuneration to be paid to the Sociedad Gestora as set forth in section III.3.2. of this 
Prospectus, in the same existing proportion, at the beginning of the immediately prior 
Interest Accrual Period, between the Mortgage Shares and all the Shares and Certificates 
included in the Fund. 
(iii) 
Payment of the net amount derived from Derivatives Contracts 1 (annual) and (biannual), 
and, in the event of termination thereof pursuant to breach by the Fund, payment of the 
amount payable by the Fund corresponding to the settlement payment.

CHAPTER VI 
GENERAL INFORMATION RELATING TO THE SOCIEDAD 
GESTORA 
 
VI.1.  Relating to the Company, Except for its Capital 
VI.1.1. 
Registered Office 
Titulización de Activos, Sociedad Gestora de Fondos de Titulización, S.A., has its registered 
office at 69, Calle Orense, Madrid. 
VI.1.2. 
Incorporation and Registration in the Registro Mercantil 
Titulización de Activos, Sociedad Gestora de Fondos de Titulización S.A., is a Spanish 
Corporation (Sociedad Anónima), with Fiscal Identification Code (CIF) A-80352750, 
incorporated on May 12th, 1992, by a deed drawn up before the Notary Public of Madrid D. 
Juan Romero-Girón Deleito, transformed into Sociedad Gestora de Fondos de Titulización 
Hipotecaria, on January 29th, 1993, in accordance with the provisions of article 6 of Law 
19/1992 of July 7th, Ley sobre Régimen de Sociedades y Fondos de Inversión Inmobiliaria y 
sobre Fondos de Titulización Hipotecaria, by virtue of the authorisation granted by Ministerial 
Order December 10th, 1992, and transformed into Sociedad Gestora de Fondos de Titulización 
by virtue of the authorisation granted by Ministerial Order February 26th, 1999. Registered with 
the Registro Mercantil of Madrid, Volume 4280, Book 0, Page 183, Section 8, Sheet M-71066, 
Registration number 5, on June 4th, 1993, and also registered with the Registro Especial de 
Sociedades Gestoras de Fondos de Titulización Hipotecaria of the Comisión Nacional del 
Mercado de Valores, under number 3. 
VI.1.3. 
Corporate Purpose 
The sole purpose of the Sociedad Gestora is the incorporation, management and legal 
representation of Fondos de Titulización de Activos and Fondos de Titulización Hipotecaria, in 
accordance with Royal Decree 926/1998, by which the Fondos de Titulización de Activos and 
Sociedades Gestoras de Fondos de Titulización are regulated. 
VI.1.4. 
Place in Which the Documents Cited in this Prospectus, or any Further Documents 
Deriving Therefrom, May be Consulted 
The Sociedad Gestora will make available, at its registered office at calle Orense 69, Madrid, to 
the public all the documents and information required pursuant to the Deed of Incorporation of 
the Fund and the present Issue Prospectus. 
Furthermore, all the information of public character described in this Prospectus will be 
available at the registered office of the Sociedad Gestora and at the Official Registry of the 
Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores.

CHAPTER VII 
MARKET CONSIDERATIONS  
VII.1.  Recent and Significant Trends of the Mortgage Market in General and of the Mortgage 
Loan Market in Particular and of the Securitization Bonds 
In recent years credit assets with mortgage guarantees in the Balance of Spanish credit entities 
have become the main protagonists of the Securitization processes of the Spanish financial system. 
On the one hand, the existence of a critical mass with the sufficient size within a subgroup of this 
type of mortgage assets has been critical: mortgage loans to private individuals to finance the 
acquisition, construction or restoration of properties. On the other, the contribution has come from 
the decisive way in which this type of financing share a series of homogeneous characteristics from 
the legal and financial points of view. 
The new legislation emerging from the Ministerial Order of May 5th, 1994, regarding the 
transparency of the financial conditions of the mortgage loans, and its subsequent development in 
the Bank of Spain Circular 5/94 of July 22nd has been one of the elements that has strengthened 
this homogeneity. 
Secondly, it is worth noting that in recent years the competition within the Spanish mortgage 
market has intensified, once private individual and credit entities have assumed the tools offered 
presented to them by Law 2/94 of March 30th, regarding subrogation and modification of the 
mortgage loans. The future influence of the announced reform of the taxation related to mortgage 
cancellation must also be added; this inevitably will also influence the rates of mortgage 
prepayment. 
Finally, the importance of the Securitized Bonds in relation to the new changes derived from the 
new mechanisms introduced by the Central European Bank in Economic Policy must be noted. 
Greater competition demands the improvement of those instruments, which allow access to 
cheaper sources of financing: instruments of issue, secondary markets, or generating techniques for 
a more efficient management of the entities’ balance. 
VII.2.  Implications Derived from those Trends Mentioned in the Preceding Section VII.1. 
The total amount of Mortgage Loans participated by the Mortgage Shares and the Mortgage 
Transfer Certificates included in TDA 22-MIXTO, Fondo de Titulización de Activos, carry a 
floating interest rate; some of which will accrue, during a transition period, at a fixed rate, such 
rates are modified periodically by variations in the interest rates of the market. Therefore, it is not 
probable that important modifications in the Prepayment Rates of the portfolio will occur due to 
changes in the interest rate levels.  
Notwithstanding the above, the average term and the duration of the issue of some Bonds in this 
Prospectus could be modified in relation to those initially estimated in section II.11. in the event 
that the Rate of Prepayment of the Shares and Certificates, varies. 
It is the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora that there is no historical public information at the 
moment regarding prepayment redemption to be able to elaborate predictions in both half and long 
term regarding the behaviour of the Prepayment Redemption Rates of the mortgage portfolios.
